         <h4 id="create-a-review-comment-for-a-pull-request-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>Multi-line comments in a pull request diff is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, these response fields may change without advance notice. See the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2019-10-03-multi-line-comments">blog post</a> for more information.</p> 
          <p>To create multi-line comments or see multi-line comments with the new supported fields during the preview period, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.comfort-fade-preview+json</code></pre> 
          <p>To show multi-line comment-supported fields in the response, use the <code>comfort-fade</code> preview header and the <code>line</code> parameter.</p> 
          <p>If you use the <code>comfort-fade</code> preview header, your response will show:</p> 
          <ul> 
           <li>For multi-line comments, values for <code>start_line</code>, <code>original_start_line</code>, <code>start_side</code>, <code>line</code>, <code>original_line</code>, and <code>side</code>.</li> 
           <li>For single-line comments, values for <code>line</code>, <code>original_line</code>, and <code>side</code> and a <code>null</code> value for <code>start_line</code>, <code>original_start_line</code>, and <code>start_side</code>.</li> 
          </ul> 
          <p>If you don't use the <code>comfort-fade</code> preview header, multi-line and single-line comments will appear the same way in the response with a single <code>position</code> attribute. Your response will show:</p> 
          <ul> 
           <li>For multi-line comments, the last line of the comment range for the <code>position</code> attribute.</li> 
           <li>For single-line comments, the diff-positioned way of referencing comments for the <code>position</code> attribute.</li> 
          </ul> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-reply-for-a-review-comment" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-reply-for-a-review-comment">Create a reply for a review comment</a> </h3> 
         <p>Creates a reply to a review comment for a pull request. For the <code>comment_id</code>, provide the ID of the review comment you are replying to. This must be the ID of a <em>top-level review comment</em>, not a reply to that comment. Replies to replies are not supported.</p> 
         <p>This endpoint triggers <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/managing-subscriptions-and-notifications-on-github/about-notifications">notifications</a>. Creating content too quickly using this endpoint may result in abuse rate limiting. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#abuse-rate-limits">Abuse rate limits</a>" and "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/guides/best-practices-for-integrators#dealing-with-rate-limits">Dealing with abuse rate limits</a>" for details.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pull_number}/comments/{comment_id}/replies</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-reply-for-a-review-comment--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-reply-for-a-review-comment--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead>

            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>pull_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td>

           </tr>

       <h2 id="review-requests"><a href="#review-requests">Review requests</a></h2> 
       <p>Pull request authors and repository owners and collaborators can request a pull request review from anyone with write access to the repository. Each requested reviewer will receive a notification asking them to review the pull request.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-requested-reviewers-for-a-pull-request" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-requested-reviewers-for-a-pull-request">List requested reviewers for a pull request</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pull_number}/requested_reviewers</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-requested-reviewers-for-a-pull-request--parameters"> <a href="#list-requested-reviewers-for-a-pull-request--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          -->

            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td>

         <h3 id="request-reviewers-for-a-pull-request" class="pt-3"> <a href="#request-reviewers-for-a-pull-request">Request reviewers for a pull request</a> </h3> 
         <p>This endpoint triggers <a href="https://docs.github.com/github/managing-subscriptions-and-notifications-on-github/about-notifications">notifications</a>. Creating content too quickly using this endpoint may result in abuse rate limiting. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#abuse-rate-limits">Abuse rate limits</a>" and "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/guides/best-practices-for-integrators#dealing-with-abuse-rate-limits">Dealing with abuse rate limits</a>" for details.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pull_number}/requested_reviewers</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="request-reviewers-for-a-pull-request--parameters"> <a href="#request-reviewers-for-a-pull-request--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>pull_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>reviewers</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>An array of user <code>login</code>s that will be requested.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_reviewers</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>An array of team <code>slug</code>s that will be requested.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="request-reviewers-for-a-pull-request--code-samples"> <a href="#request-reviewers-for-a-pull-request--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/pulls/42/requested_reviewers \
  -d '{"reviewers":["reviewers"]}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pull_number}/requested_reviewers'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">pull_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">reviewers</span>: [
    <span class="hljs-string">'reviewers'</span>
  ]
})
</code></pre>

         <h4>Unprocessable Entity if user is not a collaborator</h4>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="remove-requested-reviewers-from-a-pull-request" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-requested-reviewers-from-a-pull-request">Remove requested reviewers from a pull request</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pull_number}/requested_reviewers</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="remove-requested-reviewers-from-a-pull-request--parameters"> <a href="#remove-requested-reviewers-from-a-pull-request--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>pull_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>reviewers</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. An array of user <code>login</code>s that will be removed.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>team_reviewers</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>An array of team <code>slug</code>s that will be removed.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="remove-requested-reviewers-from-a-pull-request--code-samples"> <a href="#remove-requested-reviewers-from-a-pull-request--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X DELETE \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/pulls/42/requested_reviewers \
  -d '{"reviewers":["reviewers"]}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'DELETE /repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pull_number}/requested_reviewers'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">pull_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">reviewers</span>: [
    <span class="hljs-string">'reviewers'</span>
  ]
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 200 OK</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div>

         <pre><code>Status: 422 Unprocessable Entity</code></pre>
